- Last Updated: 2026-05-24 **(session 67 cont.11 - D-PHASE6C-WORKERAI-JOB-SPAN [S])** [HEAD `f4dc68e1`] - **Closes the Phase 6c-╬│ design ┬ž10 follow-up.** Worker-ai's `process_job` previously emitted N disconnected root traces (one per `loreweave_llm` SDK call). NEW `_with_job_span` decorator wraps each job in a single OTel parent span `worker_ai.process_job` carrying `job.{id,scope,project_id,user_id,items_total}` as attributes; the httpx instrumentor populates W3C tracecontext on outbound SDK calls so they become children of the parent span Ôćĺ Grafana Tempo shows the whole job lifecycle as one trace. Files (2): MODIFY `services/worker-ai/app/runner.py` (+`from opentelemetry import trace as _ot_trace`, +`import functools`, +module-level `tracer`, +`_with_job_span` decorator, +`@_with_job_span` on `process_job`); MODIFY `services/worker-ai/tests/test_runner.py` (+module-scoped `_worker_ai_span_exporter` fixture installing InMemorySpanExporter + rebinding `app.runner.tracer` to the test provider, +2 tests `test_process_job_emits_parent_span_with_job_attributes` and `test_process_job_span_handles_none_items_total` ÔÇö both reuse the existing `_mock_pool`/`_mock_knowledge_client`/etc. plumbing). Tests: worker-ai `test_runner.py` **40/40** pass (0.51s, was 38). **Decorator pattern chosen over in-place `with` block**: the body has ~14 inline `return` statements + an existing outer `try/except` that swallows errors, so a `try/finally` around the body would require re-indenting ~430 lines or refactoring the swallow semantic ÔÇö neither warranted for an observability enrichment. Trade-off: because the inner body swallows exceptions and calls `_fail_job` itself, the wrapper sees normal return on failed jobs and ends the span with OK status; operators investigating a failure grep logs for `job_id` to find the trace via the existing structured logger.exception. Future enrichment can have the inner signal failure via span context attribute so the wrapper sets ERROR status. **Image rebuilt + force-recreated** (worker-ai healthy + summary_consumer reconnected). **Functional live smoke** (parent span actually emitted during a job, children = SDK calls visible in Tempo) folds into the next extraction run ÔÇö unit tests prove the span emission contract; container-healthy + module-import-success is the deploy-time evidence. Memory anchors: reinforces the decorator-over-indent pattern for adding cross-cutting wrappers to large functions; `feedback_review_impl_on_design_cycles` (this was a deferred design-review item; cleared in its target follow-up).

- Last Updated: 2026-05-24 **(session 67 cont.5 - D-P3-BOOK-SUMMARY-PERSIST-AUDIT [S])** [HEAD `18a64fb1`] - **Root-cause + fix for the missing book-summary row observed in the session 67 cont.3 cascade smoke.** Stream archaeology on `extraction.summarize` (109 entries despite only 3 distinct levels per book) revealed the M4 retry mechanism was burning the entire RETRY_BUDGET=3 in milliseconds: the `if msg.retry_at_epoch > now_epoch(): await _reenqueue_with_backoff(msg)` branch in `app/jobs/summary_processor.py` re-XADDed a future-timestamped message that Redis Streams delivered immediately (no time-based delivery semantics), and the consumer picked it up, bumped retried_n + retry_at_epoch, and pushed it back ÔÇö exhausting the budget within sub-second wall-clock instead of across the intended 30+60+120s window. Higher-level summaries (book > part > chapter) hit this first because their D9 child-readiness check naturally fails on first attempt while children are still settling. Evidence: redis trail showed retried_n=0Ôćĺ1Ôćĺ2Ôćĺ3 with retry_at_epoch deltas of 30s/60s (matching REENQUEUE_BACKOFF_S = (30, 60, 120)) but the WALL-CLOCK between message creation = milliseconds. Book row only persisted at 18:00:52 ÔÇö 10m51s after the part row landed ÔÇö because a subsequent extraction trigger happened to fire AFTER the part row was already in the DB, so book D9 passed on the SECOND extraction's first attempt. Files (2 modified): MODIFY `services/knowledge-service/app/jobs/summary_processor.py` (replace the "retry_at in future Ôćĺ re-enqueue + bump retried_n" branch with `await asyncio.sleep(min(delay_s, MAX_INLINE_RETRY_SLEEP_S))` then fall through to normal processing; NEW `MAX_INLINE_RETRY_SLEEP_S = 120` constant sized to match REENQUEUE_BACKOFF_S[-1] and the worker-ai `summary_dispatch_timeout_s = 300s` HTTP budget; comment block documents the bug for future readers); MODIFY `services/knowledge-service/tests/unit/test_summary_processor.py` (REPLACE buggy-behavior-locking `test_retry_at_in_future_reenqueues_without_processing` with `test_retry_at_in_future_sleeps_then_processes_without_burning_budget` ÔÇö asserts asyncio.sleep called + summary_enqueue NOT called + processing proceeded; ADD `test_retry_at_absurd_future_sleep_capped_at_max` ÔÇö clock-skew defense regression-lock asserting sleep is capped at MAX_INLINE_RETRY_SLEEP_S even when retry_at_epoch is year-2286). First in-handoff sketch proposed a "4-tier semantic-chunking" architecture as the primary lever. User-PO rejected the framing: "viß╗çc d├╣ng SEMANTIC CHUNKING 1 c├ích m├íy m├│c l├á 1 sai lß║žm... kh├┤ng ai chß╗ë d├╣ng 1 thuß║şt to├ín ─Ĺß╗â xß╗ş l├Ż t├ái liß╗çu ÔÇö smart l├á kß║┐t hß╗úp nhiß╗üu loß║íi vß╗Ťi nhau". Cheap-first; semantic chunking is an escape valve at T2 stage 3, NOT primary. **Scale correction:** 50MB local is FEASIBLE (~24h wall-clock with checkpoint resume, parallelism=4 on local 35B); the earlier "needs cloud" claim conflated wall-clock latency with capability. Cloud is a speed-up option, not a requirement. **Roadmap:** P1 structural decomposer Ôćĺ P2 parallel map + checkpoint Ôćĺ P3 hierarchical reduce + per-level summaries Ôćĺ P4 semantic chunking escape valve Ôćĺ P5 gated LLM coref + verify + multi-res retrieval. **P1+P2+P3 alone = capability-complete for 50 MB.** Files (3): NEW `docs/03_planning/KNOWLEDGE_SERVICE_HIERARCHICAL_EXTRACTION_ADR.md` + `docs/sessions/SESSION_HANDOFF.md` (What's NEXT replaced) + `docs/sessions/SESSION_PATCH.md` (this entry). No code change in this cycle. **NEXT session:** start P1 (structural decomposer) ÔÇö multi-format parser (EPUB/MD/TEI/plain-text + Chinese/Vietnamese/English/Japanese markers) producing `StructuralTree` Pydantic schema. M cycle, no LLM, no embedding. Memory anchor (NEW): `feedback_cheap_structural_before_expensive_semantic` ÔÇö cheap deterministic decomposition before expensive probabilistic transforms; production SOTA is multi-algorithm composition.

- Last Updated: 2026-05-20 **(session 59 cycle 4 - D-EMB-MODEL-REF-04: close generic-PATCH dual-path on embedding_model [M])** [HEAD `29955655` Ôćĺ pending commit] - **D-EMB-MODEL-REF-04 closed.** The session-58 cycle-4 FE picker fix gave `ProjectFormModal` two paths to change `embedding_model`: the destructive `PUT /{id}/embedding-model?confirm=true` (deletes the graph first) AND the generic `PATCH /{id}` (which only probes the dimension). The generic path on a project with an existing graph left the old vectors in Neo4j tagged with the old model UUID while Mode-3 retrieval queried the new model's vector space ÔÇö silent zero-recall. **Fix:** added a guard in `patch_project` between the If-Match parse and the embedding-model probe ÔÇö when `embedding_model` is in `body.model_fields_set`, `repo.get` the current row (`_not_found()` if None) and reject with 422 (pointer to the destructive endpoint) if `body.embedding_model != current.embedding_model AND current.extraction_status != 'disabled'`. Guard runs BEFORE the probe so a rejection doesn't waste an `/internal/embed` round-trip. **Gate axis:** `extraction_status != 'disabled'` (Postgres-only check, leverages the natural lifecycle state ÔÇö 'disabled' = first-time setup OR post-destructive-reset). Same-value sets allowed (FE form re-submits). 3 files: `app/routers/public/projects.py` + `tests/unit/test_public_projects.py` (extended `_make_project` with `extraction_status` + `embedding_model` kwargs; +3 lock tests ÔÇö rejected-on-project-with-graph with defense-in-depth repo-state assertion, allowed-first-time-setup, same-value-noop) + SESSION_PATCH. **Pre-verified:** sibling `PUT /embedding-model?confirm=true` endpoint unchanged (its 409-for-active-jobs guard complements this 422-for-has-graph guard). **Race condition acknowledged + accepted at hobby scale:** between `repo.get` and `repo.update` a worker could flip `extraction_status` 'disabled'Ôćĺ'building'; FE picker flow doesn't realistically trigger this window; row locking is overkill. Verify: knowledge-service unit **1619/1619** (baseline 1616 + 3 lock tests); all 50 tests in test_public_projects.py green. No new deferrals filed. No /review-impl ÔÇö guard inside existing endpoint, no new abstraction.

- Last Updated: 2026-05-18 **(session 58 cycle 2 - embedding model-ref contract bug: investigation + ADR [DESIGN])** [HEAD `9eab22a2`] - **Track 2/3 extraction live-smoke attempt found a blocking cross-service contract bug; wrote an ADR, no code.** Attempting the D-K21B-06 follow-on (a live end-to-end smoke of the Track 2/3 knowledge-graph extraction pipeline) surfaced that knowledge-service passes a **logical embedding-model name** (`bge-m3`, from the `EMBEDDING_MODEL_TO_DIM` curated list) as the provider `model_ref`, but provider-registry's `POST /internal/embed` does `uuid.Parse(model_ref)` and 400s on anything non-UUID. **Every embedding call from knowledge-service is broken** ÔÇö 6 production call sites: chapter passage ingest, the live Mode-3 chat-turn query embedding (`select_l3_passages`), the K21 `memory_search` tool, drawer search, and the K17.9 benchmark (├Ś2). ## Track 2 Close-out Roadmap (session 46)

> **Why this section exists:** K18 cluster landed in session 46 (commits `d6455b8` Ôćĺ `2025951` Ôćĺ `06e5c30` Ôćĺ `d4527e0`). Mode 3 is live end-to-end, but ~24 Deferred Items remain from across the Track 2 arc. This roadmap splits them into 9 bounded cycles so each can close in a single workflow pass without the "just a bit more" scope drift that kills quality.
>
> **Rule:** cycles execute in number order by default. A higher-numbered cycle can jump ahead only if the cycles it depends on are clearly marked as done.

Review-impl added `system_prompt` as third-segment test + strengthened budget-trim test to assert trim fired.

### Cycle 8 ÔÇö Large infra (each its own cycle)
Three separate commits.

- Ôťů **8a ┬Ě D-K18.3-02** generative rerank (session 47) ÔÇö post-MMR listwise rerank via `provider_client.chat_completion` with `{"order":[int,...]}` JSON mode; opt-in via `project.extraction_config["rerank_model"]`; fail-safe fallback to MMR order on any error; inner `asyncio.wait_for(timeout=1.0s)` (review-impl catch: slow rerank was eating the 2s L3 budget and producing zero passages).
- Ôťů **8b ┬Ě D-T2-04** cross-process cache invalidation (session 47) ÔÇö new `CacheInvalidator` (publisher + subscriber on `loreweave:cache-invalidate` Redis pub/sub channel); `cache.invalidate_l0/l1/user` write paths now fire-and-forget publish after local pop; subscribers apply via `apply_remote_*` helpers (no re-publish, prevents echo storm); origin UUID per process filters self-messages; exponential-backoff reconnect; 60 s TTL still the ultimate backstop.
- Ôťů **8c ┬Ě D-T2-05** glossary breaker half-open probe (session 47) ÔÇö new `_cb_probe_in_flight` flag + `_cb_enter()` state machine returning `"closed"|"probe"|"open"`; `select_for_context` try/finally releases the probe slot under any outcome (success, failure, 4xx, decode error, unexpected exception, cancellation); atomic check-set in single-threaded asyncio guarantees exactly one probe per half-open window. Benchmark-equivalent: concurrent 5-caller test shows 1 HTTP call instead of 5 (breaker now actually breaks under load).

### Cycle 9 ÔÇö Gate-4 alignment Ôťů (session 47)
One commit.

- Ôťů **K17.9.1** `project_embedding_benchmark_runs` migration (session 47) ÔÇö new table storing K17.9 golden-set harness output keyed on `(project_id, embedding_model, run_id)` UNIQUE; `ON DELETE CASCADE` on project; covering index `(project_id, embedding_model, created_at DESC)` for the latest-run fast path; `passed BOOLEAN NOT NULL` (gate bit); `raw_report JSONB DEFAULT '{}'`; `embedding_provider_id` cross-DB (no FK). 7 unit smoke tests + 7 integration tests (incl. review-impl full-column insert + cascade-preserves-other-projects).

### Then
**Gate 13 end-to-end verification Ôćĺ Chaos tests C01ÔÇôC08 Ôćĺ Track 2 formally closed.**

**All 9 cycles of the original Track 2 close-out roadmap are complete** (session 47 shipped cycles 7a/7b/8a/8b/8c/9; cycles 1ÔÇô6 shipped in session 46). **The extended T2-close-out plan negotiated mid-session 47 is also complete** (T2-close-1a/1b-BE/1b-FE/5/6/7/3/4 + T2-polish-1/2a/2b/3; T2-close-1b-CI + T2-polish-4 scoped out by user decision; chaos C05/C06/C08 promoted to ­ččí SCRIPTED via `scripts/chaos/`). The single remaining Track 2 item is **T2-close-2** ÔÇö the human-interactive Gate 13 loop (BYOK + real project + chat turns) which can't be automated.

See [TRACK_2_ACCEPTANCE_PACK.md](TRACK_2_ACCEPTANCE_PACK.md) for the single-page Track 2 delivery evidence view.

### Summary
- **Original roadmap: 9 cycles, ~12 commits** (sessions 46 + 47)
- **Extended close-out plan: 13 cycles, 20 commits** (session 47)
- All chaos scenarios automated or scripted (C01ÔÇôC04+C07 automated unit-level; C05/C06/C08 scripted live-run one-command-away)
- Observability: /metrics now on all 3 Go services facing knowledge-service hot paths
- Track 2 code-complete; only the Gate 13 human attestation remains

Check this list at the start of every phase ÔÇö any row whose "Target phase" equals the current phase is a must-do.

> ID scheme: `D-K*-NN` = normal deferral from phase K*; `D-T2-NN` = deferred to Track 2 planning; `P-K*-NN` = perf-only, fix when profiling shows pain.

| ~~D-PHASE6A-CAP-ROUNDUP~~ | ~~session 57 cycle 3 /review-impl LOW#9~~ | **Cleared in session 67 cont.13** (3-item batch). `affordableMaxTokens` now subtracts `billing.UsdQuantum` from the budget before computing affordable output tokens, reserving headroom for the post-cap `roundUpUSD` quantum bump. NEW exported `billing.UsdQuantum` constant. Regression-lock test asserts the post-cap re-estimate (input cost + capped output, rounded to quantum) stays ÔëĄ DailyAvailable. | ÔÇö (cleared) |
| D-PHASE6A-STREAMING-GUARDRAIL | session 57 cycle 3 (design ┬ž7) | **Subsystem A is not applied to `POST /v1/llm/stream`.** Only the async job path (`doSubmitJob`) reserves. The ADR ┬ž3.4 approach for streaming stands; wire it in 6a-╬┤. | Phase 6a-╬┤ |

| D-PHASE6A-LIVE-SMOKE | session 57 cycle 3 (design ┬ž7) | **Manual smoke: a real over-budget job returns 402 end-to-end** (provider-registry Ôćĺ usage-billing, both running). Confirms the full reserve/reconcile/release loop against a live DB pair. | Phase 6a-╬┤ OR first integration-env run |
| D-PHASE6A-PRICING-FE | session 57 cycle 3 (design ┬ž7) | **Model-registration pricing form.** `user_models.pricing` is editable via the API but has no FE; users currently rely on the default price table or raw JSON. | Phase 6a-╬│ |
| D-PHASE6B-MEDIA-DOUBLE-CHARGE | session 57 cycle 7 (design ┬ž6) | **Retrying a media-gen call after an ambiguous transient error can double-generate + double-charge.** `retryTransient` retries `GenerateImage`/`GenerateVideo`/`GenerateAudio` on any transient error; if the upstream actually completed the (expensive) generation but the response was lost in transit, the retry generates again. The user chose all-transient retry at CLARIFY accepting this. A proper fix needs an idempotency key threaded through each provider adapter to the upstream. | Phase 6c+ OR when media-retry cost is observed |
| D-PHASE6B-RETRY-USAGE-DOUBLECOUNT | session 57 cycle 7 /review-impl #2 residual | **A retry can double-count usage tokens.** `chatAggregator`/`jsonListAggregator` `StartChunk` resets the per-chunk content buffer but NOT `inputTokens`/`outputTokens`; if an upstream emits a `StreamChunkUsage` chunk and then fails transiently, the successful retry re-emits usage Ôćĺ tokens summed twice. Narrow (a transient failure normally precedes the end-of-stream usage chunk) and affects both the chunked + unchunked paths. A clean fix needs per-chunk usage staging across every aggregator. | The aggregator-refactor cycle OR when billing drift is observed |
| D-PHASE6C-ALPHA-SMOKE | session 57 cycle 8 (design ┬ž9) | **Manual trace smoke ÔÇö FOUNDATION VERIFIED (session 57 cycle 8 post-cycle smoke):** both services build with the repo-root Docker context + start with `InitTracer` (healthy); SERVER spans flow service Ôćĺ collector Ôćĺ Tempo with route-pattern naming (`POST /internal/llm/jobs`, `GET /health`, `SPAN_KIND_SERVER`); a shared inbound `traceparent` JOINs into one 2-service trace (provider-registry + usage-billing); Grafana provisioned-Tempo datasource reachable. **RESIDUAL:** the full connected job trace (reserve Ôćĺ `llm.job.process` Ôćĺ reconcile Ôćĺ `llm.job.terminal-event`) needs a registered+priced model ÔÇö model-resolution gates the reserve, so a bogus `model_ref` 404s first. | First integration-env run with a registered model |

The pieces are unit-tested (`DetachedContext`, `ChiMiddleware`, `Tracer.Start`); the wiring needs a heavy `Worker` harness. | D-K19e-╬│a-02 | K19e Cycle ╬│-a /review-impl L2 (session 50) | **Drawer-search embed calls don't count toward K16.11 monthly budget.** Per-user monthly cap (session 50 D-K16.11-01 cycle) wraps the extraction worker's `_record_spending`. Drawer search fires an embedding call through the same provider-registry but bypasses that code path entirely, so power users could burn BYOK embed quota on drawer searches without the cap kicking in. At bge-m3 rates the per-search cost is ~$0.00002 ÔÇö hobby scale negligible. | D-EXTRACTION-PARALLEL-CONCURRENCY-FLAKE | session 68 /review-impl HIGH-1 root cause | **Concurrent extraction at concurrency=4 produced a transient zero-extraction on `journey_west_zh_ch01` that did not repro under isolated rerun (10 entities cleanly).** Cold-model warmup or LM Studio inter-request contention suspected. | D-AGGREGATOR-REASONING-CONTAMINATION-GUARD | session 68 /review-impl LOW-6 | **`extractJSONObject` (aggregator.go:376) assumes reasoning_content is on a separate stream channel; if a future model or LM Studio config emits reasoning as regular content tokens, the "first { to last }" boundary picks up the wrong range.** The session 68 `response_format: text` patch makes loose-output models more common downstream, raising the priority of a defensive guard. Options: pre-strip ` ```json `-fenced blocks, prefer the LAST balanced `{...}` if multiple exist, or accept the patch-by-spec assumption + add a counter for "extracted Ôëá first-brace-to-last-brace recovery" so we notice if it starts firing. | When a model emits reasoning on the content channel in practice |

| P-K19d-01 | K19d Cycle ╬▒ DESIGN (session 50) | **`list_entities_filtered` uses Cypher CONTAINS for search.** Substring scan over `name` + each alias per row. Fine at hobby scale but O(total ├Ś avg_alias_count) in worst case. Proper fix: create a fulltext index `CREATE FULLTEXT INDEX entity_name_fts FOR (e:Entity) ON EACH [e.name, e.aliases]` + switch the WHERE branch to `db.index.fulltext.queryNodes('entity_name_fts', $search)`. Mirrors the existing `entity_user_project` index for :Entity. Idempotent `IF NOT EXISTS` applies on next startup. |

### Won't-fix (conscious decisions, not debt)

- **Hard-coded English Mode-1/Mode-2 instructions.** chat-service has no i18n either ÔÇö revisit when the whole product ships i18n.
- **`loreweave_knowledge` backup script.** No backup infra for any service in Track 1 ÔÇö cross-cutting concern owned by infra, not knowledge-service.
- **K5 retry backoff between attempts.** 500ms ├Ś 2 = 1000ms total budget leaves no room for backoff. If we ever raise the timeout, revisit. Conscious decision.
- **K5 `KnowledgeClient` is a per-worker singleton.** With multi-worker uvicorn each worker has its own client + its own pool, which is correct (httpx.AsyncClient must be constructed after fork). The "singleton" is per-process, not per-cluster, by design. Not debt ÔÇö the right shape.
- **`close_knowledge_client` not guarded against concurrent calls.** Lifespan shutdown is single-threaded; not a real risk.
- **K6 glossary circuit-breaker `_cb_fail_count` drifts past threshold.** After the breaker opens at count=3, any subsequent failure that reaches `_cb_record_failure` climbs to 4, 5, ÔÇŽ Never causes incorrect behavior (count only resets to 0 on success, and the short-circuit prevents new failures from arriving in practice). Cosmetic only ÔÇö the log message `"opened after %d consecutive failures"` could over-report during a long outage. Not worth the complexity to cap.

| **D-T2-05** | **K6 (Track 2 scope since K6 commit)** | **Cleared in session 47 Cycle 8c.** `GlossaryClient` gained `_cb_probe_in_flight: bool` field + a new `_cb_enter()` state machine that returns `"closed"` (proceed), `"probe"` (this caller is the single half-open probe ÔÇö must release via `_cb_exit_probe()` in a `finally` block), or `"open"` (short-circuit). The atomic check-set inside `_cb_enter` contains no `await`, so concurrent coroutines reaching the half-open window are serialized by the event-loop scheduler ÔÇö exactly one returns `"probe"`, the rest see the flag already set and return `"open"`. `select_for_context` wraps its HTTP retry loop in `try`/`finally` so the probe slot is released under every outcome (success, 5xx failure, 4xx, decode/shape error, unexpected exception, cancellation). `_cb_record_success` also clears the flag for defense-in-depth. Benchmark validation: concurrent 5-caller test fires exactly 1 HTTP call instead of 5 (breaker now actually breaks under load). **Review-impl caught** 2 LOW items ÔÇö dead test variable + missing inline comment on the 4xx probe-release semantics ÔÇö both fixed in the same commit. +3 new tests cover concurrent serialization, probe-release after failure, and probe-release after unexpected exception; all 5 pre-existing breaker tests still pass. 1310 pass + 95 skipped. |
| **D-T2-04** | **K6 (Track 2 scope since K6 commit)** | **Cleared in session 47 Cycle 8b.** New [`app/context/cache_invalidation.py`](../../services/knowledge-service/app/context/cache_invalidation.py) holds a `CacheInvalidator` class that publishes fire-and-forget messages to a shared `loreweave:cache-invalidate` Redis pub/sub channel whenever a local `invalidate_l0 / invalidate_l1 / invalidate_all_for_user` fires. Each worker also runs a subscriber loop that consumes peer invalidations and drops the matching keys via new `apply_remote_*` helpers in `cache.py` (which DO NOT re-publish ÔÇö prevents echo storm). Per-process origin UUID (`ks-{uuid4().hex[:12]}`) filters the worker's own messages out of the subscribe stream. Subscriber has exponential-backoff reconnect (1 s Ôćĺ 10 s cap) so a Redis blip doesn't kill invalidation permanently. Publish is fire-and-forget via `asyncio.create_task` with a `_pending_publishes` set (so Python doesn't GC the task mid-send); `stop()` drains that set before closing the Redis client. Settings-gated: empty `redis_url` Ôćĺ invalidator never installs Ôćĺ Track 1 single-worker deploys stay local-only unchanged. 60 s TTL remains the backstop ÔÇö pub/sub is at-most-once, but typical staleness drops from "TTL" to "one pub/sub hop" (~1 ms). **Review-impl caught** a check-then-use race on the module-level `_invalidator` slot (local-capture fix), weak `test_start_is_idempotent` assertion (added `from_url.call_count == 1`), and missing end-to-end test of the full repoÔćĺcacheÔćĺpublish chain (added `test_repo_write_path_invokes_publish_end_to_end`). 17 tests cover publisher + subscriber + remote-apply + lifecycle. 1307 pass + 95 skipped. |

Full chain: chat Ôćĺ knowledge Ôćĺ glossary Ôćĺ book. |

## Current Active Work

### ARCH-1/2 C1+C2 ÔÇö MCP transport dual-run (session 103, arch-unify-chat-rag, FS [XL]) Ôťů

Adopted the LF-governed standard stack (MCP tool transport) per the locked design
`618bedd3` ÔÇö re-skinned the existing tool layer as MCP instead of a custom design,
because the in-repo shapes already matched (`tools/definitions` + `executor` ÔëÖ MCP
`tools/list`+`tools/call`; chat already a list+call client). **Built on Opus 4.8**
(switched mid-task ÔÇö two-service contract work warranted the stronger model).

**C1 ÔÇö knowledge-service MCP server facade.** `app/mcp/server.py` (new): FastMCP
`knowledge-memory`, all 5 memory tools (`memory_search/recall_entity/timeline/
remember/forget`) each a thin shim that builds a `ToolContext` from request headers
and delegates to the **existing** `app.tools.executor.execute_tool()` ÔÇö no logic
duplication. `_build_tool_context` derives scope (`user_id/project_id/session_id`) +
auth from headers ONLY (design D3); constant-time `secrets.compare_digest` token
check (mirrors `internal_auth.py`). Mounted `/mcp` in `main.py`; the StreamableHTTP
`session_manager.run()` runs in the lifespan (stopped BEFORE pools so in-flight calls
unwind against a still-open pool), non-fatal on startup failure Ôćĺ bespoke
`/internal/tools/*` keep serving = **dual-run**. `_dispatch` returns the bare success
payload (`result.result if not None else {}`) / `{"success":False,"error":...}` on
failure. Tool inputSchemas carry the same enums (`Literal` source_type/`FactType`
fact_type) + limit bounds (`Field(ge,le)`) as the bespoke OpenAI schema.

**C2 ÔÇö chat-service MCP client.** `knowledge_client.mcp_execute_tool()` returns the
**identical** `{success,result,error}` envelope as bespoke `execute_tool()`; binds
both `timeout` and `sse_read_timeout` to the 30s tool budget (SDK default is 300s ÔÇö
would 10├Ś the hang ceiling); forwards `X-Trace-Id`; coerces empty-successÔćĺ`{}` on
both client methods (canonical sentinel). `USE_MCP_TOOLS` gate in `stream_service`
`_stream_with_tools` (`config.use_mcp_tools=False` default) ÔÇö bespoke path stays the
live one, **zero runtime exposure** until the flag flips.

**Reviews.** Phase-7 self-review (5 LOW fixed; caught a duplicate `mcp[cli]` deps
block) Ôćĺ `/review-impl` deep pass (21 raised Ôćĺ **18 confirmed, 0 HIGH**, all fixed):
the two MED behavior bugs (timeout + trace-id drift, invisible to mock tests), the
MED boot-safety gap (`mcp>=1.9` had no ceiling + module-scope mount outside try/except
Ôćĺ pinned `,<2`), MED lifespan coverage (`test_lifespan_mcp.py` ÔÇö start/teardown
ordering + non-fatal), MED infra-error propagation pin, + LOW schema-fidelity /
real-handler success-key pins / doc notes. 3 ACCEPT_DOCUMENT (error-string wording,
transcribed-literal coupling, module-global `run()` footgun), 3 dismissed correctly.

**Files.** KS new: `app/mcp/{__init__,server}.py`, `tests/{test_mcp_server,
test_mcp_contract}.py`, `tests/unit/test_lifespan_mcp.py`; KS modified: `app/main.py`,
`requirements.txt`, `tests/unit/test_tool_executor.py`. chat new:
`tests/{test_mcp_execute_tool,test_mcp_envelope_parity}.py`; chat modified:
`app/client/knowledge_client.py`, `app/services/stream_service.py`, `app/config.py`,
`requirements.txt`. Docs: build plan, DEFERRED #056 + this entry.

**VERIFY** (independent reruns): knowledge-service **1952 passed**, chat-service
**269 passed**, 0 failed. Live cross-service smoke deferred Ôćĺ **D-ARCH2-MCP-LIVE-SMOKE**
(keep `USE_MCP_TOOLS` false until it runs).

**NEXT**: C3 (AG-UI events) Ôćĺ C4 (FE AG-UI client) Ôćĺ C5 (`<Chat>` component + editor
AI panel) Ôćĺ C6 (editor write-back / WA-4).

### K├Âppen-on-sphere spec + circulation experiment (reverted) (session 99, BE [DESIGN]) Ôťů

After the retune (above), explored candidate A (K├Âppen). PO asked the right
question ÔÇö *does the current logic actually follow the K├Âppen formula?* Honest
answer: **no**. A first circulation-bands experiment (latitude precip feeding the
`[0,1]` heuristic) **regressed** Desert to 55ÔÇô62 % because seed-7 land sits at
median |lat|Ôëł30┬░ (the dry belt) ÔÇö it modulated a proxy instead of using the real
classifier. **Reverted** `climate.rs` to the committed retune (53 %).

Wrote the full **actionable spec** instead of rushing an L climate rewrite at the
tail of a 9-commit marathon (quality-first, CLAUDE.md "don't rush"):
[`docs/specs/2026-05-30-koppen-climate-sphere.md`](../specs/2026-05-30-koppen-climate-sphere.md)
ÔÇö Option A (port the **validated** `flat_climate` K├Âppen classifier to the
sphere, keep `ClimateZone`/`BiomeKind`): real ┬░C + mm/yr derivation, the
temperature-dependent `precip < 20┬ĚT_mean+offset` aridity formula (the actual
desert fix ÔÇö hot needs ~470 mm, cold ~70 mm to escape B-group), circulation mm
curve, K├ÂppenÔćĺClimateZone map, calibrated params (T_EQ 28 / T_POLE Ôłĺ15 / precip
2400/180/900/150 / seasonal), a histogram-driven calibration plan (target Desert
30ÔÇô40 %), test rewrites, and the R6 note (sphere-native great-circle transport,
only the latitude/unit functions lifted).

**This is the de-risked plan for a focused K├Âppen build (next).** Not yet built.

### Climate audit + continentality retune (session 99, world-gen-sdk-refactor, BE [M]) Ôťů

PO picked candidate-B-then-A path. **Visual audit** of a Megaplanet (seed 7)
diagnosed the standing colour defect ÔÇö NOT "all-green" (stale) but **desert
monotony: 63 % of land was Desert, Tundra 0.1 %**. Root cause (doubt-the-
substrate): the single-direction wind `moisture_field` over-dries continental
interiors, made worse by a **resolution artifact** ÔÇö `LAND_LEAK` was a per-step
constant, so a finer mesh (Megaplanet+) accumulated more drying per geographic
unit. The biome matrix itself was fine (AridÔćĺDesert correct; PolarÔćĺTundra
correct but little polar land).

**Retune shipped (`climate.rs` only):**
- `moisture_field`: `LAND_LEAK` is now **resolution-scaled** ÔÇö
  `LAND_LEAK_BASE(0.018) * sqrt(8192/n)` clamped `[0.1,3.0]` ÔÇö so total
  continentality drying over a fixed great-circle distance is invariant across
  `WorldScale` (`OROGRAPHIC` was already invariant; climb telescopes). Lowered
  from `0.025`.
- `classify`: hot-band Arid gate `0.55Ôćĺ0.62`; warm-interior Arid override
  `0.72Ôćĺ0.80` ÔÇö Arid only when genuinely parched.

**Result: Desert 63 %Ôćĺ53 % of land**, green (forest/jungle/plain/marsh) up to
24 %, Jungle 2.6 %Ôćĺ7 %. A real incremental win + a correctness fix.

**Evidence-based finding for K├Âppen:** the cheap retune is **structurally capped
near ~50 %** ÔÇö a single-direction wind march cannot carry moisture into a huge
continent's interior from multiple sides, so the downwind Ôůö stays dry regardless
of threshold tuning. **Multi-cell circulation (candidate A / K├Âppen) is the real
fix** ÔÇö now evidence-backed, not a guess. Building it next this session.

**VERIFY:** lib **388**, climate **50**, determinism **8**, serde **5** ÔÇö 0
failed. `content_hash` re-based (run-vs-run; no literal pins). Clippy-clean.

### Session 98 ÔÇö FlatÔćĺ3D substrate audit + migration plan (PLAN only, no code) Ôťů

**Goal (PO directive end of session 97):** discussion+plan, no code. Audit whether
the flat-map civ experiment will make the eventual "elevation map applied at the
end" a painful retrofit.

**Key finding (lesson 1fbf8d34 applied):** the PO's fear is largely already
resolved, but not as expected. The civ stack (`political`/`settlement`/`routes`/
`culture`/`feature`/`naming`/`hydrology`) is **mesh-agnostic shared modules** ÔÇö
sphere `generate()` (lib.rs:100-124) calls the *same* functions `civ_adapter.rs`
(civ_adapter.rs:47-51) calls. The sphere substrate **already has** real 3D
elevation (plate tectonics + Earth-like hypsometry + erosion since Phase 1). The
flat track is an **experiment**; its missing elevation is experiment-only, not a
pending production retrofit.

**Genuinely flat-only:** `flat_climate` 5-layer K├Âppen/Whittaker (21-cell, richer
than sphere's 8-zone); the hierarchical zone tree (plateÔćĺzoneÔćĺsubzone); the 2D
shape dispatcher (coupled to 2D geometry, won't transfer). The 3 hardcoded LLM
provider files (`shape/{anthropic,ollama,openai}.rs`) only survive on
`civ-layer-amaw` ÔÇö PR #13 deleted them for the SDK gateway.

**Decisions:** sphere = production substrate; flat = frozen + harvested (its one
real win, layered climate, becomes the documented Phase 3 K├Âppen work if/when
shipped). No civ feature exempt from running on the sphere (lesson b720b779).

**PO picks (session 98):** next-ship = **candidate C3** ÔÇö lift the hierarchical
hierarchy to the sphere, **geometric frame first** (C-1: continents Ôćĺ
subcontinents Ôćĺ regions) then **political tiers** (C-2: world Ôćĺ realm Ôćĺ nation Ôćĺ
province Ôćĺ county). Multi-session XL arc toward the MMO end-state.

**Output doc:** [`docs/03_planning/LLM_MMO_RPG/FLAT_TO_3D_MIGRATION_PLAN.md`](../03_planning/LLM_MMO_RPG/FLAT_TO_3D_MIGRATION_PLAN.md)
ÔÇö honest current state, Q1-Q6 audit, migration decisions, C3 arc breakdown,
risk register (R1-R7).

**C-1 DESIGN completed in-session (PO said continue).** Investigated real code:
the hierarchy is mostly REUSE of existing primitives ÔÇö `pathfind::land_components`
(continents, already used by political.rs:29), `feature::components` (ocean
basins), `plates.plate_of` (subcontinents = continentÔłęplate). Only L2 regions are
new (great-circle Voronoi, copy plates.rs:99-114 pattern). D1-D4 all resolved
(┬ž7 of migration doc). C-1 split into C-1a (model, M) + C-1b (render, S) per PO.

**Next (session 99 = BUILD, C-1a, size M):** geometric hierarchy MODEL only,
NO render. New WorldMap fields continent_of/subcontinent_of/region_of + vecs;
L2 region-count knob on CreativeSeed; pin re-based content_hash. VERIFY must
assert partition invariants (no orphan cells, regionÔŐćsubcontinentÔŐćcontinent),
not just serialization. Traps: R6 (3D great-circle Voronoi, not 2D grid), R7
(reuse plates/land_components, no parallel partition). Then C-1b render, then
C-2 political tiers (re-anchor province under region).

**Files touched:** 1 new doc + this SESSION_PATCH entry. No code. No tests run
(plan session). No commit unless PO requests.

### Phase A v4.1a ÔÇö Tier 3 zone templating SCHEMA (session 67, geo-generator-amaw, BE [XL staged 1/4]) Ôťů

Driver: roadmap ┬ž4 Tier 3 row v4.1 (highest-risk phase per roadmap ┬ž10, 5/5 risk, 14-18h estimate). PO chose STAGED migration at CLARIFY (v4.1a schema only Ôćĺ v4.1b climate Ôćĺ v4.1c render Ôćĺ v4.1d cleanup) to reduce per-cycle risk. This is ship 1 of 4 for the Tier 3 zone-templating roadmap row.

- Files touched (2 code):
  - `crates/world-gen/src/flatworld.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö NEW `Zone` struct (id, plate_id, center, components: Vec<Polygon>, size_rank, shape_seed, shape_kind) + `Plate.zones: Vec<Zone>` field. `flatworld::generate` populates `plate.zones` via dispatcher at `depth=1` per existing `plate.zone_sites` entry (zone_sites is preserved for backward compat). `derive_zone_rank` helper maps plate rank Ôćĺ zone rank (GiantÔćĺMedium / LargeÔćĺMedium / MediumÔćĺSmall / SmallÔćĺSmall / MicroÔćĺMicro) so zone polygons stay proportional. Default dispatcher upgraded to `PerDepth([Weighted(engine_v3_6_weights()), Random, Random])` ÔÇö PerDepth at depth=0 delegates to Weighted with zero RNG overhead, preserving plate byte-identical contract. Zone-level v3.5 coastline fractalize runs on each zone polygon (PO #3 universal-fractalize choice). Entity path string for zones is `"plate.{p}.zone.{z}"` (Manual override key format consistent with v4.0). Test helpers updated with `zones: Vec::new()`.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/flatworld.rs` tests (MOD) ÔÇö 4 new v4.1a tests: zones populated for every plate, zones have valid polygons (Ôëą1 component, Ôëą3 vertices, archipelago-tolerant), varied shape kinds across zones, default dispatcher is `None` (so PerDepth wrap fires).

- Tests: **315/315 pass** (was 311 at v4.0; +4 v4.1a tests). Clippy: 3 pre-existing warnings (BLEND_TEMP / BLEND_PRECIP / doc indent); 0 new from v4.1a.

- Hash pins SURVIVE ÔÇö v4.1a is **schema-additive** ship. `Plate.zone_sites` and `Plate.subzone_sites` are STILL populated (backward compat); rendering / climate / hydrology consumers still read from those Voronoi seed points. Biome + hypso pixel hash unchanged.

- PO staged-migration plan:
  - **v4.1a (this ship)**: schema only ÔÇö `Plate.zones` populated as templated polygons; consumers untouched.
  - **v4.1b**: migrate `flat_climate.rs` consumers (`compute_zone_climate` uses `plate.zones[zi].center` and `plate.zones[zi].components` instead of `zone_sites[zi]`).
  - **v4.1c**: migrate `zonegen.rs` rendering (per-zone polygon paint instead of Voronoi).
  - **v4.1d**: drop `zone_sites` field + `subzone_sites` (v4.2 owns subzone templating).

- Key BUILD discoveries (RETRO):
  1. **PerDepth([Weighted, Random, Random]) preserved plate byte-identicality.** Verified hash pin survival: PerDepth at depth=0 delegates with zero RNG overhead, so plate generation is bit-identical to v3.6. PerDepth's value as forward-compat scaffolding from v4.0 paid off immediately in v4.1a.
  2. **Multi-component zone polygons require archipelago-tolerant tests.** Japan stamp's 4-arc emits at zone scale Ôćĺ `ctx.center` lands at "sea" between islands Ôćĺ naive `zone.contains(zone.center)` returns false. Slime's agent walks similarly drift. Test relaxed to assert polygon validity instead of centre containment ÔÇö the climate/render code uses point-in-polygon over ALL components anyway, so the strict invariant doesn't help v4.1b/c consumers.
  3. **Backward-compat dual-field schema decouples ship cycles.** Keeping `zone_sites` alongside `zones` means v4.1b can migrate one consumer at a time without breaking the others. Less risky than big-bang refactor; total cycle count + LOC is higher but each cycle is testable.

- Workflow gate phases passed (all 12, default v2.2 mode): CLARIFY Ôćĺ DESIGN Ôćĺ REVIEW(design) Ôćĺ PLAN Ôćĺ BUILD Ôćĺ VERIFY Ôćĺ REVIEW(code) Ôćĺ QC Ôćĺ POST-REVIEW. SESSION + COMMIT + RETRO closing now.

- Phase A v4.1a CLOSED (ship 1 of 4 for Tier 3 zone templating). Next ship in the staged sequence: **v4.1b** climate migration (`flat_climate.rs` reads from `plate.zones[zi].center` + iterates `plate.zones[zi].components`).

### Phase A v4.0 ÔÇö Tier 2 Dispatcher Refactor (session 66, geo-generator-amaw, BE [L]) Ôťů

Driver: roadmap ┬ž6 ÔÇö Tier 2 starts the dispatcher's evolution from "pick a kind" into the full multi-mode selector that supports PO override (Manual), rule-based context dispatch (ByContext), LLM-driven selection (Llm ÔÇö deferred to v4.3 per PO directive), and the per-depth + fallback-chain combinators that v4.1/v4.2 zone templating will rely on.

- Files touched (3 code):
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/dispatch.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö `DispatchMode` enum extended with 5 new variants: `Manual(HashMap<String, ShapeKind>)`, `ByContext(Vec<ContextRule>)`, `Layered(Vec<DispatchMode>)`, `PerDepth([Box<DispatchMode>; 3])`, `Llm` (stub). NEW `ContextPredicate` enum with `Any` / `Rank` / `Depth` / `LatBand { min, max }` atoms plus `And` / `Or` / `Not` boolean combinators. NEW `ContextRule { predicate, kind }`. `select()` signature gains `entity_path: &str` param. Internal `select_opt()` returns `Option<ShapeKind>` so Layered detects abstain Ôćĺ fall through. Public `select()` always commits via Random fallback when every layer abstains. Llm variant panics with explicit v4.3 ship message.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/flatworld.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö caller updated to pass `entity_path = "plate.{id}"`.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/dispatch.rs` tests (MOD) ÔÇö 8 new tests covering Manual lookup + fall-through, ByContext rule fire, Layered fall-through chain + Manual-first-wins precedence, PerDepth depth indexing, ContextPredicate And/Or/Not composition, Llm stub panic via `#[should_panic(expected = "v4.0 stub")]`.

- Tests: **311/311 pass** (was 303 at v3.6; +8 dispatcher tests). Clippy: 3 pre-existing warnings (BLEND_TEMP / BLEND_PRECIP / doc indent); 0 new from v4.0.

- Hash pins SURVIVE ÔÇö this is API-level extension only. Default `FlatParams.plate_dispatch = None` still routes through `Weighted(engine_v3_6_weights())` byte-identical to v3.6. No render comparison needed.

- PO CLARIFY decisions:
  1. **LLM cache postponed to v4.3** ÔÇö PO observed `eval/llm_shape_cache.json` from roadmap ┬ž8 doesn't fit the platform architecture (cloud-hosted MMO with shared DB/Redis). v4.0 ships Llm variant as panic stub; v4.3 ships full LLM dispatch + cache architecture decision (Postgres vs file vs none vs endpoint-side caching like Anthropic prompt caching) together.
  2. **Path-based string keys for Manual** ÔÇö `HashMap<String, ShapeKind>` with `"plate.{id}"` keys (v4.1+ will add `"plate.{id}.zone.{id}"`). Caller in flatworld.rs constructs the key.
  3. **User-config `Vec<DispatchMode>` for Layered** ÔÇö full PO control over fallback chain order. Layered iterates in caller-supplied order.
  4. **Hybrid NL+JSON prompt format** documented for v4.3 ÔÇö system prompt = natural language guidance, user prompt = JSON ShapeContext, JSON-schema-constrained reply parses to ShapeKind.

- Architecture clarification logged: world-gen is currently a STANDALONE CLI tool. When integrated into the MMO platform (per CLAUDE.md `services/` Postgres/Redis/MinIO), cache layer moves to shared storage. v4.0 doesn't commit to either local-file or cloud-DB cache ÔÇö v4.3 decides with full context.

- Key BUILD discoveries (RETRO):
  1. **`select_opt` Option-returning internal API is the keystone of Layered.** Once internal select can "abstain" (Manual: no entry; ByContext: no matching rule), the Layered combinator is a 4-line iter. The public `select` keeps the always-committing contract via a final Random fallback.
  2. **`PerDepth` is forward-compat scaffolding.** v4.0 only exercises depth=0 (plates) since v4.1 zone templating hasn't shipped. But the variant + dispatch logic is in place so v4.1 doesn't need to retrofit; just wire `PerDepth([plate_mode, zone_mode, subzone_mode])` and it works.
  3. **PO caught an architecture mismatch at CLARIFY.** Roadmap ┬ž8 spec'd a local cache file without thinking through the multi-user MMO platform layer. PO redirected Ôćĺ v4.0 ships stub + defers decision. Lesson: spec sections written for CLI tools may not fit production-platform architecture; flag and re-decide when integration looms.
  4. **`entity_path` was the minimal-invasive way to add identity to dispatch.** Alternatives (add `id: usize` to ShapeContext + change every generator) would have been schema-touching. Passing a string from the caller is opaque to generators but visible to Manual lookup ÔÇö clean separation.

- Workflow gate phases passed (all 12, default v2.2 mode): CLARIFY Ôćĺ DESIGN Ôćĺ REVIEW(design) Ôćĺ PLAN Ôćĺ BUILD Ôćĺ VERIFY Ôćĺ REVIEW(code) Ôćĺ QC Ôćĺ POST-REVIEW. SESSION + COMMIT + RETRO closing now.

- Phase A v4.0 CLOSED. Tier 2 dispatcher refactor SHIPPED. Llm variant deferred to v4.3 with cache architecture decision. Next: **v4.1 Tier 3 zone templating** (Plate.zones: Vec<Zone> replaces zone_sites Voronoi) ÔÇö highest-risk phase per roadmap ┬ž4 (5/5 risk; 14-18h; touches climate + drainage + render). Or revisit Llm v4.3 if PO wants LLM integration sooner.

### Phase A v3.5 ÔÇö Coastline Fractalize (session 64, geo-generator-amaw, BE [L]) Ôťů

Driver: PO redirect during v3.4 POST-REVIEW ÔÇö "real coastlines are not straight lines, like the Mandelbrot coastline paradox" ÔÇö replaced original v3.5 scope (stamps library) with **universal fractalize post-process** that applies Hausdorff-1.25 coast detail to every plate polygon regardless of which generator made it.

- Files touched (4 code + 1 spec + 1 baseline + 18 PNGs):
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/coastline.rs` (NEW) ÔÇö ~280 LOC. `FractalizeConfig` struct (roughness/iterations/perlin_freq/apply_to_satellites) + `fractalize_polygon` hybrid algorithm. Stage A: midpoint displacement with `0.5^iter` amplitude decay (PO-approved at CLARIFY) ÔÇö each iteration roughly doubles vertex count via perpendicular-offset midpoint insertion. Stage B: per-vertex 2D fbm Perlin warp via `crate::noise::fbm` for micro-detail. 6 unit tests (disabled config = clone, 0 iterations = clone, count doubling, determinism, roughness scaling, warp preservation).
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/mod.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö `pub mod coastline` + re-exports `FractalizeConfig`, `fractalize_polygon`.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/flatworld.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö NEW `FlatParams.coastline: FractalizeConfig` field (default = roughness 0.35, iterations 3, perlin_freq 8.0, apply_to_satellites true). Post-process hook in `generate()` after each generator returns `ShapeResult`: fractalize primary + optionally satellites. Internal RNG via `Rng::for_stage(shape_seed, b"coastline")` so caller stream invariance is preserved.
  - `crates/world-gen/examples/flatworld.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö NEW CLI flags `--coastline-roughness <0..1>`, `--coastline-iter <0..5>`, `--coastline-enabled <0|1>`.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/zonegen.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö hash pins biome + hypso rebased v5.6 with v3.5 rationale comment.
  - `docs/specs/2026-05-28-flatworld-v3-5-coastline-fractalize.md` (NEW) ÔÇö spec with all 12 ┬ž5 acceptance criteria.
  - `eval/baselines/v5.8.json` (NEW) ÔÇö composite 81.87 baseline.
  - `eval/compare-v3-5/` (NEW dir) ÔÇö 18 PNG artifacts (5 default seeds + 4 chaos-sweep at seed 42, plates + biome each).
  - `docs/plans/2026-05-25-phase-a-v3-roadmap.md` (MOD) ÔÇö ┬ž13 extended with 10-item **natural-fragmentation enhancements** list per PO directive (water/wind/tectonic break-up for future Phase B+ / V5 implementation).
  - `docs/deferred/DEFERRED.md` (MOD) ÔÇö NEW #026 umbrella entry indexing the 10 enhancements.

- Tests: **295/295 pass** (was 289 at v3.4, +6 new for coastline). Clippy: 3 pre-existing warnings (BLEND_TEMP / BLEND_PRECIP / doc indent); 0 new from v3.5.

- Test adaptations:
  - `flatworld_v3_0_byte_identical_seeds_1_7_13_42_100` ÔÇö explicitly sets `coastline: FractalizeConfig::disabled()` to preserve v3.0 byte-identical hash invariants.
  - `phase_a_defaults_use_high_vertex_count` ÔÇö disables coastline so the generator's own vertex-count fit is asserted directly (post-fractalize count can be 8├Ś the input range per PO CLARIFY decision: vertex_count_range is GENERATOR contract, not final).
  - Hash pins biome + hypso rebased v5.5 Ôćĺ v5.6 (coastline modifies every plate polygon at the seed-7 96├Ś64 hash-pin world).

- Eval: composite **77.30 Ôćĺ 81.87 (+4.57 IMPROVEMENT)** ÔÇö fractal coast detail counter-balances v3.4 slime cost by adding biome-band smoothing (coast detail effectively softens lat-band transitions). 9 of 11 renders improved Ôëą1.0. Only baseline_s42 regressed (-7.30). scenario_desert +7.86 (largest gain). v5.8.json locked.

- Phase A composite progression: v3.1c 80.89 Ôćĺ v3.2 84.70 (+3.81) Ôćĺ v3.3 84.61 (-0.09) Ôćĺ v3.4 77.30 (-7.31) Ôćĺ **v3.5 81.87 (+4.57)**. Net Phase A delta: +0.98 with 7 generators + fractal coast + multi-component support.

- Visual journey (single round, no rework):
  - `--coastline-roughness 0.0` = same as v3.4 (smooth polygonal coasts).
  - `--coastline-roughness 0.35` (default) = recognisable but moderate fractal coast detail across all generators.
  - `--coastline-roughness 0.7` = heavy fractal, peninsulas + bays everywhere.
  - `--coastline-roughness 1.0` = extreme, coast starts fragmenting (self-intersecting). Default sweet spot at 0.35.

- Key BUILD discoveries (RETRO):
  1. **Single integration point in `flatworld::generate` was clean.** Considered making fractalize a `ShapeGenerator` wrapper or per-generator hook, but the simplest path ÔÇö wrap the generator output in `flatworld::generate` ÔÇö works for all 7 generators with zero per-generator code changes.
  2. **Vertex-count contract clarification.** Pre-v3.5 `ctx.vertex_count_range` was both the generator's output target AND the final polygon count. With fractalize ON the count can grow 8├Ś post-process. PO ruled this is fine ÔÇö vertex_count_range is the GENERATOR contract; the final polygon is whatever the post-process produces. Test adapts.
  3. **Eval improved despite extra vertex chaos.** Counter-intuitive: fractal coastlines INCREASED composite by +4.57. Reason: smoother biome-band transitions at the coast (more vertices = more sampling resolution = softer ecotones in `lat_banding`).
  4. **PO mid-roadmap idea-capture pattern.** During v3.5 POST-REVIEW PO added "water/wind/erosion break-up" as a FUTURE 10-item list. Logged to roadmap ┬ž13 + DEFERRED #026 instead of expanding v3.5 scope. Cleaner: ship the working feature, log the next ideas for their dedicated cycle.

- Workflow gate phases passed (all 12, default v2.2 mode): CLARIFY Ôćĺ DESIGN Ôćĺ REVIEW(design) Ôćĺ PLAN Ôćĺ BUILD Ôćĺ VERIFY Ôćĺ REVIEW(code) Ôćĺ QC Ôćĺ POST-REVIEW. SESSION + COMMIT + RETRO closing now.

- Phase A v3.5 CLOSED. Next: v3.6 (or v4.0 if stamps deferred indefinitely) ÔÇö original v3.5 stamps library OR v4.0 dispatcher refactor (LLM mode / Manual mode / Layered fallback). Roadmap ┬ž4 Tier 1 fully shipped (all 7 algorithms + fractal coast).

### Phase A v3.4 ÔÇö Slime / Physarum + concave hull (session 63, geo-generator-amaw, BE [L]) Ôťů

Driver: roadmap ┬ž4 Tier 1 v3.4 ÔÇö first emergent / agent-based shape generator (multi-agent walk + concave hull, modelled after biological slime mold + DBM lightning physics per research ┬ž1). PO directive at CLARIFY (maximal-thoroughness per user memory): hybrid tunable per template (Blob single, Branch multi-eligible); aggressive agent budget; hybrid ╬▒-shape primary + Moreira-Santos fallback.

- Files touched (6 code + 1 spec + 1 baseline + 18 PNGs):
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/slime.rs` (NEW) ÔÇö ~830 LOC. Multi-agent walk (per-template `energy` + `step_size_factor` for SlimeBlob vs SlimeBranch). ╬▒-shape primary via `delaunator::triangulate` + circumradius filter (╬▒ = avg_spacing ├Ś 1.8 ÔÇö tighter wrap than the initial 2.5 multiplier after PO's "nh├Čn qu├í ch├ín" feedback in round 2). Moreira-Santos k-nearest concave hull fallback for cases where ╬▒-shape can't recover a usable boundary. Quality filter: if total area < target ├Ś 0.25, retry with XORed seed up to 3├Ś then fall back to Ellipse with honest `effective_kind = Ellipse`. Multi-comp filter per template (Blob keeps largest only; Branch keeps primary + satellites Ôëą 1% bbox). 2-pass Chaikin + DP simplify (eps = 0.15% diag) + shape-preserving vertex-count fit so output lands in `ctx.vertex_count_range`.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/dispatch.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö NEW `engine_v3_4_weights()` restoring Slime per-rank weights (G/L/M=0.05, S/╬╝=0.10) per roadmap ┬ž14 Q4. `engine_default()` now registers 7 generators (adds SlimeGenerator). Updated test `engine_default_v3_4_registers_seven_kinds`.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/mod.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö re-exports `SlimeGenerator`, `SlimeTemplate`, `engine_v3_4_weights`.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/csg.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö Boolean WedgeCut template's wedge vertex moved from (0, 0) Ôćĺ (0.5, 0); EllipseDifference inner ellipse moved from (0.5, 0.2)/0.6├Ś0.5 Ôćĺ (0.6, 0.25)/0.45├Ś0.4 so the subtracted region no longer covers origin. Defensive Ellipse fallback when result polygon doesn't contain `ctx.center`. Caught when v3.4 dispatcher RNG shift pushed WedgeCut into plate 8 at default seed and `plate.contains(plate.center)` failed.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/flatworld.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö default dispatch flipped from `engine_v3_2_weights` Ôćĺ `engine_v3_4_weights`. `engine_v3_1b/v3_2_weights` retained as `pub` for reproducing older baselines.
  - `crates/world-gen/examples/flatworld.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö `--force-kind` accepts `slime`.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/zonegen.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö hash pins biome + hypso rebased v5.5 with v3.4 rationale comment.
  - `docs/specs/2026-05-27-flatworld-v3-4-slime-physarum.md` (NEW) ÔÇö spec with all 13 ┬ž5 acceptance criteria + 3 BUILD rounds documented.
  - `eval/baselines/v5.7.json` (NEW) ÔÇö composite 77.30 baseline.
  - `eval/compare-v3-4/` (NEW dir) ÔÇö 18 PNG artifacts (5 default seeds ├Ś {plates, biome} + 4 Fixed-slime seeds ├Ś {plates, biome}).

- Tests: **289/289 pass** (was 281 at v3.3, +8 net: 8 slime tests ÔÇö walk determinism + bounds + ╬▒-shape disk recovery + Moreira-Santos sparse cloud + 4 generator integration).
  Clippy: 3 pre-existing warnings (BLEND_TEMP / BLEND_PRECIP / doc indent); 0 new from v3.4.

- Eval: composite **84.61 Ôćĺ 77.30 (-7.31)**. 7 of 11 renders regress >5 points (scenario_desert -17.29 largest; baseline_s7 / hemi_eq / hemi_north / hemi_south / baseline_s99 / scenario_hothouse all -8 to -13). Intrinsic cost of slime shapes: blob+branch silhouettes span more lat bands than ellipse/spine shapes, hurting `lat_banding`. Per PO directive ┬ž14 Q6 (eval is tool not gate): regression accepted. v4.5 calibration phase will retune metrics. 2 renders improved Ôëą1.0.

- 3 build rounds:
  1. Round 1: initial spec + slime.rs at PO-approved aggressive params (6-8 agents ├Ś 8000 steps). Result: agents saturated bounds rectangle, ╬▒-shape recovered the bbox ÔÇö plates rendered as overlapping rectangles. BAD.
  2. Round 2: per-template tuning ÔÇö Blob (6 agents ├Ś 900 steps ├Ś persistence 0.30 ├Ś step target_r/30), Branch (8 agents ├Ś 400 steps ├Ś persistence 0.85 ├Ś step target_r/87). Organic shapes appeared but PO feedback: "nh├Čn qu├í ch├ín" (too boring ÔÇö under-detailed crude blobs).
  3. Round 3: visual tightening ÔÇö ╬▒ multiplier 2.5 Ôćĺ 1.8 (tighter wrap captures inlets/peninsulas), Chaikin 1 Ôćĺ 2 passes (smoother but more detail), DP eps 0.5% Ôćĺ 0.15% diag (preserves more vertices), 3000-anchor subsample cap (was 1500), shape-preserving vertex-count fit so output respects `ctx.vertex_count_range`. Result: organic continents with tendrils, bays, scattered island chains ÔÇö visually convincing slime mold output.

- Key BUILD discoveries (RETRO):
  1. **PO-approved "aggressive" params can be wrong.** PO chose aggressive 6-8 agents ├Ś 8000 steps at CLARIFY without seeing visual impact. At plate scale (envelope=234) the agents traveled ~13k units and saturated the bounds box. Lesson: validate spec parameters against a sample render BEFORE locking acceptance criteria; CLARIFY answers from PO are intent not engineering correctness.
  2. **Boolean WedgeCut template was always broken** ÔÇö wedge vertex at origin meant the Pac-Man bite went through plate centre. Test never caught it because v3.2 dispatcher RNG sequence never picked WedgeCut at default seed (plate 8). v3.4 dispatcher RNG shift exposed the latent bug. Lesson: hash-pin tests + center-containment tests catch correctness AT specific seeds; algorithmic templates need their own correctness audits independent of which seeds happen to exercise them.
  3. **╬▒-shape multiplier is the dominant visual-quality knob.** ╬▒/avg_spacing = 2.5 Ôćĺ 1.8 took slime from "boring blobs" to "organic continents". Smaller ╬▒ = tighter local wrap = preserves concave detail. Going too small (< 1.2) starts excluding interior triangles and producing holes ÔÇö a future v3.5+ knob.
  4. **PO redirect mid-roadmap: v3.5 = fractalize coastline.** Original v3.5 was "stamps library" but PO asked about Mandelbrot coastline paradox during v3.4 POST-REVIEW; redirected v3.5 to universal fractal coastline post-process (hybrid midpoint displacement + Perlin warp). Stamps deferred to v3.6 or later.

- Workflow gate phases passed (all 12, default v2.2 mode): CLARIFY Ôćĺ DESIGN Ôćĺ REVIEW(design) Ôćĺ PLAN Ôćĺ BUILD Ôćĺ VERIFY Ôćĺ REVIEW(code) Ôćĺ QC Ôćĺ POST-REVIEW. SESSION + COMMIT + RETRO closing now.

- Phase A v3.4 CLOSED. Next: v3.5 ÔÇö **fractalize coastline** (hybrid midpoint displacement + Perlin warp, universal post-process across all plate generators) per PO mid-roadmap redirect.

### Phase A v3.3 ÔÇö Multi-component plates / true archipelagos (session 62, geo-generator-amaw, BE [L]) Ôťů

Driver: roadmap ┬ž4 Tier 1 v3.3 ÔÇö lift the v3.2 `largest_ring()` restriction so MarchingNoise can produce multi-component archipelagos (Indonesia / Japan / Philippines-style island groups). PO directive at CLARIFY: hybrid primary+satellite schema (primary owns Voronoi zones, satellites visual-only); all applicable gens (MarchingNoise + Boolean + SDF) eligible; no count cap, 1% bbox area filter.

- Files touched (5 code + 1 spec + 1 baseline + 14 PNG):
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/raster.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö `field_to_polygon` signature lifted to `Vec<Polygon>` with new `min_area_frac: f32` param. NEW `finalize_multi_component` (always-keep-primary + filter satellites by area threshold). **MarchingNoise totally redesigned** to multi-island generator: N=2-6 island seed centres placed via Poisson-disk rejection (45% separation gap), per-island Pareto-weighted size weights Ôćĺ radii from area share, per-island noise warp (3-octave fbm, different salt per island). +2 new raster tests (two-disks Ôćĺ 2 polys, tiny island below threshold dropped).
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/sdf.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö caller updated to new field_to_polygon API + min_area_frac=0.01. SDF templates stay single-component in practice (chain topology shares joints).
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/csg.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö `safe_union` / `safe_difference` refactored to return `Vec<GeoPolygon>` sorted by area; `sort_or_fallback` replaces `largest_or_fallback`. NEW `filter_pieces_by_area` (primary always kept + 1% threshold). NEW `fit_piece_to_envelope_shared` (shared bbox + combined max_dist across pieces; single-piece byte-identical to v3.2 ÔÇö verified by hash pin survival).
  - `crates/world-gen/src/flatworld.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö NEW `v3_3_default_renders_have_multi_component_plate` regression test (forced `Fixed(MarchingNoise)` verifies fragmentation at Ôëą1 of 5 seeds).
  - `crates/world-gen/examples/flatworld.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö NEW `--force-kind <ellipse|bezier|polar|boolean|sdf|marching>` CLI flag for visual QC of individual generators.
  - `docs/specs/2026-05-27-flatworld-v3-3-multi-component.md` (NEW) ÔÇö spec with all 12 ┬ž6 acceptance criteria + 4 BUILD rounds documented.
  - `eval/baselines/v5.6.json` (NEW) ÔÇö composite 84.61 baseline.
  - `eval/compare-v3-3/` (NEW dir) ÔÇö 14 PNG artifacts (5 default seeds ├Ś {plates, biome} + 4 Fixed-MarchingNoise seeds ├Ś {plates, biome}).

- Tests: **281/281 pass** (was 280 at v3.2, +1 net for v3.3 acceptance test).
  Clippy: 3 pre-existing warnings (BLEND_TEMP / BLEND_PRECIP / doc indent); 0 new from v3.3.

- Eval: composite **84.70 Ôćĺ 84.61 (-0.09 flat)**. Only baseline_s99 regresses -1.53 (acceptable per PO ┬ž14 Q6: eval is tool not gate). All other renders byte-identical or near-flat. Hash pins biome + hypso both survive (single-piece paths byte-identical to v3.2).

- 4 build rounds (compressed from 1 spec'd round):
  1. Round 1: lift largest_ring restriction, naive noise field tune (amp 0.3 Ôćĺ 0.55). PO requested aggressive noise; observation: single-blob with fringe satellites.
  2. Round 2: amp Ôćĺ 0.7. PO diagnosed correctly: "archipelago is not a shape, it is a group of shapes" ÔÇö fundamentally one-blob algorithm couldn't produce real archipelago.
  3. Round 3: total redesign ÔÇö N=2-6 island seed centres each with own SDF disk + noise. Multi-component visible but islands often overlapped (sticking together).
  4. Round 4: Poisson-disk rejection sampling with 45% separation gap. Islands now properly scatter with sea between them.

- Key BUILD discoveries (RETRO):
  1. **"1 noise field around 1 center" is fundamentally not an archipelago generator.** Even at max noise amplitude it produces a perturbed blob, not separated islands. Need N distinct seed centres each with own field component Ôćĺ `min()` SDF combine.
  2. **Poisson-disk rejection sampling cleanly controls island spacing.** Pre-compute per-island radii from Pareto-weighted area share, then place centres one-by-one rejecting any within `(r_i + r_j) ├Ś (1 + gap)` of existing islands. 24-try retry + graceful fallback to last candidate if rejection saturates.
  3. **csg.rs `fit_piece_to_envelope_shared` must use `combined_max_dist`** (not bbox half-diagonal). Half-diagonal made single-piece Boolean plates shrink by ~20%, hash pins drifted, eval regressed -14pt at baseline_s7. Switching to true max-vertex-distance restored byte-identical single-piece behaviour.
  4. **MarchingNoise dispatcher rate is too low for organic multi-comp visibility at default seeds** (G=0.10/L=0.10/M=0.05 Ôćĺ avg 0.45 plates/render Ôćĺ 10% chance of zero picks at 5 seeds). Verification uses `Fixed(MarchingNoise)` to test CAPABILITY not density. Weight rebalancing deferred to v3.4/v3.5 ship cycle.

- Workflow gate phases passed (all 12, default v2.2 mode): CLARIFY Ôćĺ DESIGN Ôćĺ REVIEW(design) Ôćĺ PLAN Ôćĺ BUILD Ôćĺ VERIFY Ôćĺ REVIEW(code) Ôćĺ QC Ôćĺ POST-REVIEW. SESSION + COMMIT + RETRO closing now.

- Phase A v3.3 CLOSED. Next: v3.4 ÔÇö Slime / Physarum agent walk + concave hull (per roadmap ┬ž4 Tier 1).

### Phase A v3.2 ÔÇö SDF capsule chain + marching squares (session 61, geo-generator-amaw, BE [XL]) Ôťů

Driver: roadmap ┬ž4 Tier 1 v3.2 ÔÇö extend the 4-algorithm v3.1 dispatcher with 2 new shape kinds whose topologies the spline-based generators can't produce cleanly. SdfCapsuleChain owns branching (Y / crab / worm); MarchingNoise owns noise-field continents. Both share a 256├Ś256 marching-squares raster pipeline.

- Files touched (8 code + 2 docs + 1 baseline + 10 PNGs):
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/raster.rs` (NEW) ÔÇö 600 LOC (320 code + 200 tests + 13 tests). `field_to_polygon` generic over `Fn((f32,f32)) -> f32`: grid sample Ôćĺ marching squares (16-case lookup + saddle disambiguation via cell-centre sample) Ôćĺ contour stitch via `BTreeMap<EdgeId, Vec<usize>>` (deterministic) Ôćĺ largest ring by signed area Ôćĺ Chaikin ├Ś 2 Ôćĺ Douglas-Peucker simplify Ôćĺ shape-preserving vertex-count fit (re-DP eps growth + edge subdivision) Ôćĺ centroid alignment (skipped when target already inside polygon) Ôćĺ CCW orientation. `MarchingNoiseGenerator` impl uses `crate::noise::fbm(p ├Ś freq, salt, 3)` + radial falloff.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/sdf.rs` (NEW) ÔÇö 410 LOC (260 code + 150 tests + 6 tests). `sdf_capsule` + Qu├şlez `smin_poly` primitives. `CapsuleTemplate::{YBranch, ZZigzag, CrabRadial, WormChain}` with per-template joints / edges / radii / smin_k. `SdfCapsuleChainGenerator` picks template by `Rng::for_stage(seed, b"sdf-capsule-chain")` (caller RNG untouched).
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/dispatch.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö `engine_v3_2_weights()` returns full PO-approved 6-kind per-rank table (spec ┬ž4.6); `ShapeRegistry::engine_default()` extended to register SdfCapsuleChain + MarchingNoise; 4 new tests.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/shape/mod.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö re-exports the 2 new generators + `engine_v3_2_weights` + `CapsuleTemplate`.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/flatworld.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö default dispatch flipped from `Weighted(engine_v3_1b_weights())` to `Weighted(engine_v3_2_weights())`; `engine_v3_1b_weights` preserved as `pub` for reproducibility; NEW `v3_2_default_renders_use_new_shape_kinds` regression test (seeds 13/42/108/256/512 each must show Ôëą1 SDF/Marching plate).
  - `crates/world-gen/src/flat_climate.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö `orographic_reduces_precip_behind_mountains` switched from custom (plates=5, seed=7) config to default 12-plate world ÔÇö small config no longer guarantees an upwind-of-mountain zone under v3.2 shape distribution.
  - `crates/world-gen/src/zonegen.rs` (MOD) ÔÇö hash pins for biome + hypso renders rebased to v5.4 (df1d6b0a... and ba0993ff...) with v3.2 rationale comment.
  - `docs/deferred/DEFERRED.md` (MOD) ÔÇö D025 logged: lat_banding entropy rewrite deferred to v4.5 calibration (PO-approved at design review).
  - `docs/specs/2026-05-26-flatworld-v3-2-sdf-marching.md` (NEW) ÔÇö v3.2 spec with all 12 ┬ž7 acceptance criteria.
  - `docs/plans/2026-05-26-flatworld-v3-2-implementation.md` (NEW) ÔÇö implementation plan.
  - `eval/baselines/v5.5.json` (NEW) ÔÇö composite 84.70 baseline.
  - `eval/compare-v3-2/` (NEW dir) ÔÇö 10 PNG artifacts (seeds 13/42/108/256/512 ├Ś {plates, biome}).

- Tests: **278/278 pass** (was 253 at v3.1c, +25 net: 13 raster + 6 sdf + 4 dispatch + 1 flatworld acceptance + 1 sdf saddle determinism). Clippy 3 pre-existing warnings (BLEND_TEMP / BLEND_PRECIP / doc indent in flat_climate.rs); 0 from v3.2.

- Eval: composite **80.89 Ôćĺ 84.70 (+3.81 IMPROVEMENT)**. 9 of 11 renders improved Ôëą1.0; 2 minor regressions (s13 -2.97, s42 -2.73). No regression >3 pts. v5.5.json locked.

- Key BUILD discoveries:
  1. **Marching-squares lookup table had 6 case-orientation bugs** in initial draft (3 non-saddle + 3 saddle sub-cases ÔÇö masks 0b1011, 0b1101, 0b1110, plus 2 saddle sub-cases of 0b0101 and 0b1010). Discovered when plate 1 polygon at default seed showed self-intersection (v18 cut across center). Each case is now annotated inline with its CCW orientation logic.
  2. **`align_centroid` must skip when target is already inside polygon** ÔÇö for non-convex Y-branch / CrabRadial shapes the polygon centroid can sit in a concave gap *outside* the polygon. Forcing alignment moves the polygon away from `ctx.center`. The SDF / noise field encoding already centers the shape, so alignment is only needed as a fallback.
  3. **Vertex-count clamp must be shape-preserving** ÔÇö arc-length resampling from ~250 vertices to ~28 cut concave corners on Y-branch / Crab shapes. Replaced with: if over-max re-run DP with geometrically-growing eps; if under-min subdivide longest edges (insert midpoints ÔÇö preserves shape exactly).

- Workflow gate phases passed (all 12, default v2.2 mode): CLARIFY Ôćĺ DESIGN Ôćĺ REVIEW(design) Ôćĺ PLAN Ôćĺ BUILD Ôćĺ VERIFY Ôćĺ REVIEW(code) Ôćĺ QC Ôćĺ POST-REVIEW. SESSION + COMMIT + RETRO closing now.

- Phase A v3.2 CLOSED. Roadmap ┬ž4 Tier 1 row v3.2 done. Next: v3.3 (multi-component plates via marching squares ÔÇö true archipelagos, 6-8h, XL-ish).

### LM-STUDIO-URL-FIX ÔÇö provider-registry adapter strips trailing /v1 from base URL (session 52, BE [M]) Ôťů
### C-P1-STRUCTURAL-DECOMP - P1 structural decomposer (hierarchical extraction T1) (session 62, XL) Ôťů

First implementation phase of the session-61 hierarchical extraction ADR. Replaces the naive `splitChapters` (`<h1>` Ôćĺ fallback `<h2>` Ôćĺ fallback single chapter; DOCX always 1 chapter) with a multi-format, multi-language **structural decomposer** that emits a 4-level tree (`book Ôćĺ part Ôćĺ chapter Ôćĺ scene`). P2 (parallel map + checkpoint), P3 (hierarchical reduce + per-level summaries) ÔÇö the two phases that, with P1, give 50MB-novel local capability ÔÇö remain.

- **CLARIFY (PO answers)**: owner = book-service domain (worker-infra path + book-service `.txt` sync path); formats = EPUB + DOCX + Markdown + plain-text EN/CN/VN/JP; per-chapter glossary anchor = P2 concern (out of P1); stack = Python SDK `loreweave_parse`; persistence = full `parts`/`scenes` Postgres schema in P1 (no two-step refactor); PDF deferred.
- **DESIGN**: [`docs/specs/2026-05-23-p1-structural-decomposer.md`](../specs/2026-05-23-p1-structural-decomposer.md) ÔÇö 10 design decisions D1-D10. D1 Python SDK hosted via knowledge-service `/internal/parse` (one HTTP hop instead of in-process). D2 parts+scenes tables in book-service DB with `lifecycle_state`/`parse_version`/`trashed_at`/`updated_at`. D3 pandoc HTML for EPUB/DOCX/MD via worker-infra + book-service synchronous `.txt` via `/internal/parse` (H1 fix ÔÇö the old `.txt` short-circuit bypassed worker-infra entirely). D4 HTML walker locked to `BeautifulSoup(html, "html.parser")` + `<body>`-only walk + h1=part/h2=chapter/h3=scene + `<hr/>` scene break + `html_to_leaf_text` algorithm pinned. D5 plain-text regex sets per language, whole-line anchored (M3 fix ÔÇö rejects `"I. understand"` mid-paragraph), scene break allows space-separated marks. D6 `/internal/parse` 200MiB body cap + OTel `parse.structural_decomposition` span + 400/413/422/500. D7 3-level Tx scoping in worker-infra import_processor + book-service processTxtImport (per-part single INSERT + per-chapter Tx grain preserved). D8 StructuralTree Pydantic with invariants. D9 ZERO LLM/embedding calls (asserted by `test_sdk_has_no_outbound_http_imports`). D10 `parse_version int` on parts + scenes for re-parse capability.
- **REVIEW (design)**: 3 self-review findings (R-SELF-1 backfill source mismatch ÔÇö switched to NULL `structural_path` sentinel + no backfill; R-SELF-2 Tx regression ÔÇö restored per-chapter Tx grain; R-SELF-3 sort_order book-global preserves existing unique index). Then `/review-impl` round 1: 3 HIGH (H1 .txt bypass, H2 HTMLÔćĺtext algorithm not locked, H3 `/internal/parse` body cap missing) + 7 MED (M1 pandoc wrapper handling, M2 EPUB nav dropped for P1, M3 Roman regex over-match, M4 parser library not locked, M5 lifecycle parity, M6 P2 fallback contract, M7 rate-limit deferred) + 4 LOW + 1 COSMETIC. All HIGH+MED actionable folded inline; 2 MED deferred (M7 + L1 streaming).
- **PLAN**: [`docs/plans/2026-05-23-p1-structural-decomposer.md`](../plans/2026-05-23-p1-structural-decomposer.md) ÔÇö 25 file touches mapped (10 NEW + 8 MODIFY + 1 DELETE-symbols + 6 NEW-test), 10 fixture corpora enumerated (L2 resolved), 6-step DAG with commit grain, migration sequence with rollback, test sequencing, 4 implementation questions for BUILD.
- **BUILD (5 steps, 5 commits planned)**: **Step 1** SDK loreweave_parse with `_types.py` + `_text_strip.py` + `html_walker.py` + `plaintext_parser.py` + `dispatcher.py` + `__init__.py` + parent `pyproject.toml` registration + `bs4>=4.12` dep. Mid-build SDK test failures uncovered 4 categories of bugs (inline-element newline pollution in `get_text(separator="\n")` Ôćĺ rewrote `_text_strip.py` to walk BLOCK_TAGS innermost-only; part/chapter regexes over-matched body lines starting with `"Part 1 "` or `"šČČńŞÇšźáŃü«"` Ôćĺ tightened to `(?:\s+[^.\n]*)?$` whole-line tail; VI scene-break `[ÔÇô-]{3,}` didn't match space-separated `"ÔÇô ÔÇô ÔÇô"` Ôćĺ allowed both consecutive + space-separated; detect_language tie-break used alphabetical lang string Ôćĺ switched to dict-insertion-order). Final **SDK 35/35** green. **Step 2** `/internal/parse` router on knowledge-service + 9 router tests + main.py wire-up + requirements.txt bs4 + config `max_parse_body_bytes`. **Step 3** book-service migrate.go: parts + scenes tables + ALTER chapters; 5 regression-lock tests including idempotency. **Step 4** worker-infra parse_client.go + import_processor.go 3-level Tx rewrite + DELETE splitChapters/splitOnH1/splitOnTag/extractFirstHeading/h1Re/h2Re/Chapter/section. parse_client_test.go (6 tests) including X-Internal-Token regression-lock per `feedback_mock_only_coverage_hides_crossservice_bugs` memory. **Step 5** book-service parse.go (parseClientCall + processTxtImport with 3-level Tx) + import.go `.md` format + `.txt` branch routed through processTxtImport per H1; 6 tests.
- **VERIFY**: SDK 35/35 + knowledge-service unit suite 1654/1654 (+ 9 new from baseline 1620 + sdks editable picked up via `pip install -e .`) + worker-infra tasks green + book-service api+config+migrate green. Pre-existing `TestLoadDefaults` panic in worker-infra/config/config_test.go confirmed NOT P1 via git stash + retest; filed D-WORKER-INFRA-CONFIG-TEST. **Live infra unavailable**: `docker compose build knowledge-service` fails repeatedly with pip `JSONDecodeError: Unterminated string` during requirements.txt install (3 retries; book-service Go rebuild succeeded Ôćĺ not P1 code). Cross-service live smoke deferred via D-P1-LIVE-SMOKE per CLAUDE.md soft-WARN rule.
- **REVIEW (code) /review-impl round 2**: 0 HIGH + 4 MED + 5 LOW + 3 COSMETIC. Fix-now batch (~25 LoC): M1 `html_to_leaf_text` direct-text fallback for nested-list / loose-text in containers + 2 regression-lock tests; L1 `_PATTERNS` dict-order regression-lock test; L2 OTel `leaf_max_chars` attribute per spec D6; M2 inline doc on `chapter_raw_objects` semantic change with cross-ref to D-P1-CHAPTER-RAW-AUDIT; C1+C3 consistent per-part indexing in multi-part filenames + dropped redundant `storage_key` per-chapter-suffix concat (UUID alone provides uniqueness). SDK 35Ôćĺ38 (+3 for M1+L1). All other suites re-green.
- **QC**: ADR ┬ž7 P1 acceptance ÔÇö multi-format parser YES, StructuralTree YES, marker detection per language YES, ZERO LLM/embedding YES, 10 fixture corpora PARTIAL (SDK-internal HTML+plain fixtures cover the algorithm; explicit 10 corpora deferred to live smoke), real EPUB integration test DEFERRED via D-P1-LIVE-SMOKE. 4/6 pass + 2 deferred-via-row.
- **POST-REVIEW**: presented summary including 6 deferred rows + verify evidence + known gaps; PO approved.
- **Files (25):** NEW `sdks/python/loreweave_parse/{__init__.py,_types.py,_text_strip.py,html_walker.py,plaintext_parser.py,dispatcher.py}` (6) + `sdks/python/tests/test_loreweave_parse_{html_walker,plaintext,roundtrip}.py` (3) + MODIFY `sdks/python/pyproject.toml`; NEW `services/knowledge-service/app/routers/internal_parse.py` + `tests/unit/test_internal_parse.py` + MODIFY `app/main.py` + `app/config.py` + `requirements.txt`; NEW `services/worker-infra/internal/tasks/parse_client.go` + `parse_client_test.go` + MODIFY `internal/tasks/import_processor.go` + `internal/tasks/html_to_tiptap.go` + `internal/tasks/html_to_tiptap_test.go` + `internal/config/config.go`; NEW `services/book-service/internal/api/parse.go` + `parse_test.go` + MODIFY `internal/api/import.go` + `internal/config/config.go` + `internal/migrate/migrate.go` + NEW `internal/migrate/migrate_test.go`. Plus `docs/specs/2026-05-23-p1-structural-decomposer.md` + `docs/plans/2026-05-23-p1-structural-decomposer.md`.
- **Memory anchors:** `feedback_cheap_structural_before_expensive_semantic` (validated ÔÇö pandoc + structural walk handle every fixture without semantic chunking), `feedback_review_impl_on_design_cycles` (round 1 caught 3H+7M at DESIGN, round 2 caught 4M post-BUILD ÔÇö pattern continues to pay), `feedback_design_test_plan_is_a_checklist` (caught the M3 gap ÔÇö promised processImport integration tests weren't written Ôćĺ D-P1-IMPORT-PROCESSOR-INTEG-TESTS), `feedback_mock_only_coverage_hides_crossservice_bugs` (parse_client_test.go explicitly assert X-Internal-Token header per D-CHAT-BILLING-01 pattern).
